Heart Disease Meal Plan (Indian)

Keywords:

heart, hypertension, coronary artery disease, atrial fibrillation, angina, peripheral artery disease, thrombosis, aneurysm, arrhythmia

Weekly Meal Plan:

Monday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Oats Upma with plenty of vegetables
2. Besan Chilla with mint chutney
3. Multigrain Daliya (Broken wheat) porridge with skimmed milk

Lunch Options:
1. Roti (2), Palak Paneer (low fat), Salad
2. Brown Rice, Dal Tadka (less oil), Roasted Bhindi
3. Millet Rotis (Jowar/Bajra), Methi Aloo (baked), Curd

Dinner Options:
1. Moong Dal Khichdi with vegetables
2. Grilled Fish (Indian spices) with stir-fried greens
3. Pumpkin Soup, Multigrain Toast, Sauteed Beans

Snack Options:
1. Roasted Makhana (Fox nuts)
2. Fruit Chaat (Papaya/Pomegranate)
3. Buttermilk with roasted cumin

Tuesday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Idli (2) with Sambar and Coconut Chutney (mild)
2. Ragi Dosa with Vegetable Stew
3. Vegetable Poha with peanuts and lemon

Lunch Options:
1. Chapati (2), Rajma Masala, Cucumber Raita
2. Quinoa Pulao with mixed veggies and Curd
3. Jowar Roti, Baingan Bharta, Salad

Dinner Options:
1. Vegetable Oats Soup, Sprouted Moong Salad
2. Chicken Curry (home style, less oil), Brown Rice
3. Bottle Gourd (Lauki) Sabzi, Phulka (2)

Snack Options:
1. Walnuts and Almonds
2. Sprouts Chaat
3. Green Tea with roasted Chana

Wednesday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Methi Thepla (low oil) with Curd
2. Vegetable Omelette (egg whites) with Multigrain Toast
3. Suji Upma with peas and carrots

Lunch Options:
1. Brown Rice, Fish Curry (Indian style), Cabbage Sabzi
2. Missi Roti, Lauki Kofta (steamed), Salad
3. Chapati, Chana Masala, Buttermilk

Dinner Options:
1. Dalia Khichdi with spinach
2. Paneer Tikka (grilled), Green Salad
3. Vegetable Clear Soup, Soy Bean Sabzi

Snack Options:
1. Guava slices with chaat masala
2. Flaxseeds and Pumpkin seeds mix
3. Roasted Masala Papad (microwave)

Thursday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Vermicelli (Semiya) Upma with lots of veggies
2. Mung Bean Dosa (Pesarattu) with ginger chutney
3. Apple and Cinnamon Porridge (Oats/Dalia)

Lunch Options:
1. Bajra Roti, Sarson Ka Saag (less ghee), Salad
2. Curd Rice with Pomegranate and tadka
3. Chapati, Mushroom Masala, Dal Fry

Dinner Options:
1. Tomato Soup, Grilled Chicken Breast
2. Tinda Sabzi, Phulka, Dal
3. Stir-fried Broccoli and Tofu

Snack Options:
1. Roasted Peanuts (unsalted)
2. Orange or Sweet Lime
3. Murmura (Puffed Rice) Bhel with veggies

Friday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Paneer Bhurji with Toast
2. Adai (Mixed Lentil Dosa) with Tomato Chutney
3. Corn Flakes with Skimmed Milk and Almonds

Lunch Options:
1. Roti, Bhindi Masala, Dal Tadka
2. Lemon Rice, Sambar, Beetroot Poriyal
3. Chicken Curry, Brown Rice, Cucumber Salad

Dinner Options:
1. Masoor Dal Soup, Grilled Fish
2. Palak Khichdi
3. Mixed Vegetable Curry, Ragi Roti

Snack Options:
1. Carrot sticks with Hummus
2. Boiled Egg whites
3. Tender Coconut Water

Saturday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Stuffed Paratha (Gobi/Mooli) - roasted, low oil, with Curd
2. Appam with Vegetable Stew
3. Oats Idli with Sambar

Lunch Options:
1. Chapati, Egg Curry, Salad
2. Bisibelebath (with brown rice and veggies)
3. Multigrain Roti, Matar Paneer, Raita

Dinner Options:
1. Lemon Coriander Soup, Grilled Paneer
2. Turai (Ridge Gourd) Sabzi, Phulka
3. Baked Chicken Tandoori style, Salad

Snack Options:
1. Roasted Chana (Chickpeas)
2. Watermelon cubes
3. Tea with Marie biscuit

Sunday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Misal Pav (use sprouts, less oil)
2. Dhokla with Green Chutney
3. Fruit Salad with Yogurt and Flaxseeds

Lunch Options:
1. Vegetable Biryani (less oil), Raita, Salan
2. Fish Fry (Shallow fried/baked), Rasam, Rice
3. Chole, Bhatura (Baked/Air-fried) or Kulcha, Salad

Dinner Options:
1. Pumpkin Soup, Sautéed Mushrooms
2. Dal Makhani (Low fat cream/milk), Jeera Rice
3. Mixed Vegetable Salad with Tofu

Snack Options:
1. Popcorn (homemade, low salt)
2. Handful of roasted seeds
3. Vegetable Juice (Carrot-Beetroot)

Recommended Foods: Spinach (Palak), Methi, Fish (Rohu/Salmon), Garlic, Flaxseeds, Oats, Millets

Unrecommended Foods: Deep fried snacks (Samosa/Pakora), High salt pickles, Ghee-laden sweets

Thursday:

Breakfast Options:

Lunch Options:
1. Brown Rice, Vegetable Stir-fry (Indian style)

3. Scrambled Egg with spinach

Lunch Options:
1. Vegetable Pulao with Soybean chunks
2. Chapati, Cauliflower Sabzi, Dal
3. Fish Curry, Rice, Cucumber Salad

Dinner Options:
1. Turkey/Chicken Meatballs, Whole wheat pasta
2. Vegetable Stew, Appam
3. Dal Soup, Sautéed Beans

Snack Options:
1. Sliced apple with almond butter
2. Sprouts Chaat
3. Turmeric Milk

Sunday:

Breakfast Options:
1. Smoothie bowl with nuts and seeds
2. Paneer Paratha (Low oil) with Curd
3. Oats Uttapam

Lunch Options:
1. Quinoa Bowl with Rajma and Avocado
2. Chapati, Sarson ka Saag, Salad
3. Chicken Biryani (Home cooked, less oil), Raita

Dinner Options:
1. Baked Fish with steamed asparagus
2. Vegetable Soup, Moong Dal Cheela
3. Tinda Sabzi, Phulka

Snack Options:
1. Popcorn (plain/turmeric)
2. Fruit Salad
3. Buttermilk

Recommended Foods: Turmeric (Haldi), Ginger, Garlic, Cruciferous veggies (Gobi/Broccoli), Berries, Green Tea

Unrecommended Foods: Processed meats, Deep fried Indian snacks, Sugary mithai, Alcohol

Unrecommended Foods: Alfalfa sprouts (Can trigger flare), Garlic (Boosts immune system too much for some), Saturated fats, Processed foods.
